	<body>
		<category name="Revolvers (Jakobs Barrel Version)">
			<category name="Description">
				<comment>By Aaron0000</comment>
				<comment>Features:</comment>
				<comment>Changes the Jakobs pistol barrel to behave like the Revolvers of Borderlands 1. Includes options for turning many pistols in the game into Revolvers (and turns Gwen's Head into the Borderlands 1 Anaconda), which are off by default.</comment>
				<comment>High damage.</comment>
				<comment>High accuracy.</comment>
				<comment>+100% critical hit damage.</comment>
				<comment>Lowered fire rate.</comment>
				<comment>Lowered reload speed.</comment>
				<comment>Recoil is larger.</comment>
				<comment>Consumes 3 ammo per shot (Maliwan consumes 4 per shot.)</comment>
				<comment>Typically six shots, can be higher or lower depending on manufacturer/grip/accessory/rarity.</comment>
				<comment>NOTES:</comment>
				<comment>If using the Luck Cannon, there is a revolver fix for it at the bottom.</comment>
				<comment>If using S&S Forever (not S&S Lite), these is a revolver fix for it at the bottom.</comment>
				<comment>If using the Defiler (my version), there is a revolver fix for it at the bottom.</comment>
				<comment>If using Atlas Reborn's Aries, there is a revolver fix for it at the bottom.</comment>
				<comment>If using the Cyber Eagle, there is a revolver fix for it at the bottom.</comment>
				<comment>If using the Discipline, there is a revolver fix for it at the bottom.</comment>
				<comment>Credits;</comment>
				<comment>Koby, for letting me use his Revolver Law.</comment>
			</category>
			<category name="Code">
